## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[getEtaTranslation called] --> B{Check eta value}
    B -->|PENDING_DISPATCH| C{Has date range?}
    C -->|Yes| D[Return formatted date range]
    C -->|No| E[Return simple dispatch text]
    B -->|DELAYED_PENDING_PICKUP| F[Return delayed pickup text]
    B -->|DELAYED| G[Return delayed text]
    B -->|TBD| H[Return TBD text]
    B -->|HOLD| I[Return hold text]
    B -->|TBD_ON_HOLD| J[Return TBD on hold text]
    B -->|DELIVERED| K[Return delivered text]
    B -->|TBD_PENDING_UPFIT_COMPLETE| L[Return upfit pending text]
    B -->|default| M[Return original eta]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    N[getEtaTooltipTranslation called] --> O{Is FreightVerify ETA?}
    O -->|Yes| P[Return FV calculation tooltip]
    O -->|No| Q{Check eta value}
    Q -->|PENDING_DISPATCH| R[Return pending dispatch explanation]
    Q -->|DELAYED_PENDING_PICKUP or DELAYED| S[Return delayed in network explanation]
    Q -->|TBD or HOLD or TBD_ON_HOLD| T[Return no updates explanation]
    Q -->|default| U[Return null]
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> PENDING_DISPATCH
    PENDING_DISPATCH --> DELAYED_PENDING_PICKUP
    PENDING_DISPATCH --> TBD
    DELAYED_PENDING_PICKUP --> DELAYED
    TBD --> TBD_ON_HOLD
    TBD --> HOLD
    TBD --> TBD_PENDING_UPFIT_COMPLETE
    DELAYED --> DELIVERED
    TBD_PENDING_UPFIT_COMPLETE --> DELIVERED
    HOLD --> DELIVERED
    TBD_ON_HOLD --> DELIVERED
    DELIVERED --> [*]
```
